# OpenAlternativeLearn

Open-source alternatives with Codex courses and interactive classrooms.

A curated awesome-list of open-source alternatives, extended with Codex HTML courses and interactive classroom previews.

Website: [https://open.aiflowlearn.net](https://open.aiflowlearn.net)

## AI & Machine Learning

### AI Development Platforms

- [Open Mercato](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/open-mercato) - A modular CRM/ERP framework built on Next.js and TypeScript that encodes hundreds of architectural decisions so dev teams can ship production features in days, not months. Alternative to SAP, Retool. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/open-mercato/open-mercato)
- [Parlant](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/parlant) - A conversational AI server that manages agent behavior through context-aware guidelines, keeping responses consistent, auditable, and aligned at scale. Alternative to Voiceflow, Chatbase, Uchat. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/emcie-co/parlant)
- [ACI.dev](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/aci-dev) - Platform for connecting AI agents to 500+ tools with built-in multi-tenant auth management and granular permissions using either function calling or a unified MCP server Alternative to Pipedream, Eden AI, Rube. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/aipotheosis-labs/aci)
- [Agenta](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/agenta) - Open-source LLMOps platform providing prompt management, evaluation, and observability tools for building robust AI applications with team collaboration. Alternative to LangSmith, Humanloop. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/agenta-ai/agenta)
- [AgentOS](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/agentos) - Open-source TypeScript runtime for autonomous AI agents with cognitive memory, multi-agent orchestration, runtime tool generation, and support for 21 LLM providers. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/framersai/agentos)
- [Agno](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/agno) - Open-source platform that enables developers to create, deploy and monitor AI agents with built-in memory, knowledge integration, and external tool connectivity. Alternative to Kiro, LangChain, Humanloop. [`Course`](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/codex/agno-agi-agno) `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/agno-agi/agno)
- [Arize Phoenix](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/arize-phoenix) - Open-source platform for LLM tracing, evaluation, and optimization. Features automatic instrumentation, prompt playground, and real-time AI application monitoring. Alternative to LangSmith, LangChain, Humanloop. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/arize-ai/phoenix)
- [Beam](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/beam) - Run AI workloads with sub-second cold starts, elastic GPU scaling, and secure sandboxed environments. Scale to zero when idle, burst to thousands instantly. Alternative to Together Sandbox, Vertex AI, Modal. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/beam-cloud/beta9/)
- [Bifrost](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/bifrost) - Open-source AI gateway delivering 50x faster performance than alternatives. Access 1000+ models from 8+ providers with built-in governance, fallback, and observability. Alternative to Eden AI, OpenRouter, Vercel AI Gateway. [`Course`](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/codex/bifrost) `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/maximhq/bifrost)
- [Botpress](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/botpress) - A comprehensive platform for creating AI agents with intuitive tools, extensive integrations, and enterprise-grade features powered by the latest language models. Alternative to Manychat, Voiceflow, Uchat. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/botpress/botpress)
- [ByteChef](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/bytechef) - Create intelligent automation workflows combining AI agents with your favorite apps and services. Connect, automate, and scale your operations without complex coding. Alternative to n8n, Make, Zapier. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/bytechefhq/bytechef)
- [CodeZero](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/codezero) - Open-source no-code automation platform for logistics, chatbots, and AI agents. Deploy on cloud, self-host, or hybrid with complete data sovereignty and modular workflow design. Alternative to Zoho Flow, Azure Logic Apps. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/code0-tech/codezero)
- [CopilotKit](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/copilotkit) - Integrate production-ready AI copilots into any product quickly and easily with CopilotKit's open-source platform. [`Course`](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/codex/copilotkit-copilotkit) `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/CopilotKit/CopilotKit)
- [Daytona](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/daytona) - Elastic sandbox infrastructure for running AI-generated code with sub-90ms environment creation, stateful operations, and isolated execution across Python, TypeScript, Go, and more. Alternative to Together Sandbox, Modal, Sprites. [`Course`](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/codex/daytonaio-daytona) `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/daytonaio/daytona/)
- [Dify](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/dify) - Visual platform for building agentic workflows, RAG pipelines, and LLM-powered apps. Supports hundreds of models, MCP integration, and self-hosted deployment. Alternative to Glide, Retool, Humanloop. [`Course`](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/codex/dify-llm-workflow-platform) [`Classroom`](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/classroom/dify) [Repo](https://github.com/langgenius/dify)
- [E2B](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/e2b) - Provide AI agents with secure, isolated sandboxes featuring real-world tools, code execution, and enterprise-grade security. Trusted by 88% of Fortune 100 companies. Alternative to Together Sandbox, Modal, Sprites. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/e2b-dev/e2b)
- [Envoy AI Gateway](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/envoy-ai-gateway) - Open source gateway built on Envoy for routing application traffic to GenAI services. Supports 16+ LLM providers including OpenAI, Anthropic, AWS Bedrock. Alternative to Eden AI, Vercel AI Gateway, Cloudflare AI Gateway. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/envoyproxy/ai-gateway)
- [FastGPT](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/fastgpt) - FastGPT is a free, open-source platform for creating AI-powered knowledge bases with data processing, model invocation, and visual workflows. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/labring/fastgpt)
- [Flowise AI](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/flowise-ai) - Open source platform for building AI agents, chatbots, and multi-agent systems using a drag-and-drop interface, with support for 100+ LLMs and RAG. Alternative to n8n, Make, Power Apps. [`Course`](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/codex/flowiseai-flowise) [`Classroom`](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/classroom/flowise-ai) [Repo](https://github.com/flowiseai/flowise)
- [Giselle](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/giselle) - Create powerful AI agents using an intuitive node-based interface that connects multiple LLMs and data sources for automated documentation and development workflows. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/giselles-ai/giselle)
- [Grepture](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/grepture) - An AI gateway that sits on the request path to handle PII redaction, prompt injection blocking, tracing, evals, and cost tracking for OpenAI, Anthropic, and Gemini. Alternative to Vercel AI Gateway, Cloudflare AI Gateway, Kong AI Gateway. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/grepture/proxy)
- [Laminar](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/laminar) - Laminar is an open-source platform that helps collect, understand, and utilize data for building high-quality LLM applications. Alternative to LangChain, Pinecone. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/lmnr-ai/lmnr)
- [Langflow](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/langflow) - Build, deploy, and iterate on AI agents, RAG applications, and MCP servers using a drag-and-drop visual interface backed by Python. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/langflow-ai/langflow)
- [Langfuse](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/langfuse) - Langfuse provides tracing, evaluations, prompt management, and analytics to debug and improve LLM applications. Alternative to LangSmith, LangChain, Humanloop. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/langfuse/langfuse)
- [Latitude](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/latitude) - Traces AI agents in production, automatically clusters failures into issues, generates evals from real failures, and alerts you when something breaks or regresses. Alternative to LangSmith, Humanloop, Weights. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/latitude-dev/latitude-llm)
- [Letta](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/letta) - Letta is an open-source platform for creating AI agents with built-in memory, reasoning, and support for thousands of tools. Alternative to Perplexity, LangChain, Pinecone. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/letta-ai/letta)
- [LibreChat](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/librechat) - Chat with multiple AI providers through a single self-hostable interface, with support for custom agents, file uploads, plugins, and multi-user access control. Alternative to Claude, Grok, ChatGPT. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/danny-avila/librechat)
- [LiteLLM](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/litellm) - Acts as a unified proxy across 100+ LLMs, normalizing them to the OpenAI format while handling virtual keys, budgets, rate limits, fallbacks, and cost tracking. Alternative to LangChain, Eden AI, OpenRouter. [`Course`](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/codex/berriai-litellm) `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/berriai/litellm)
- [LLM Gateway](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/llm-gateway) - Route, manage, and analyze LLM requests across multiple providers with one API. Compatible with OpenAI format, includes usage analytics and performance monitoring. Alternative to Eden AI, Vercel AI Gateway, Cloudflare AI Gateway. [`Course`](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/codex/llm-gateway) `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/theopenco/llmgateway)
- [LobeChat](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/lobechat) - A collaborative platform to create, schedule, and operate AI agents that handle long-running tasks, team workflows, and automated jobs without constant oversight. Alternative to Claude, Grok, ChatGPT. [`Course`](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/codex/lobe-chat-multi-agent) `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/lobehub/lobe-chat)
- [Mem0](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/mem0) - Adds persistent, searchable memory to AI agents and apps, so they remember user preferences and past interactions across sessions without pipeline changes. Alternative to LangChain, Pinecone, Vertex AI. [`Course`](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/codex/mem0-ai-memory-layer) [`Classroom`](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/classrooms/7bed9716-ba55-4442-b3f3-3cbb22343d0a) [Repo](https://github.com/mem0ai/mem0)
- [Milvus](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/milvus) - Open-source vector database optimized for similarity search, scaling to billions of vectors with minimal performance loss Alternative to Supabase, Pinecone, ElasticSearch. [`Course`](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/codex/milvus-io-milvus) `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/milvus-io/milvus)
- [Multica](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/multica) - Open-source platform that manages coding agents as team members, with task queues, skill libraries, runtime monitoring, and a unified activity feed. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/multica-ai/multica)
- [Nango](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/nango) - Complete integrations platform with 500+ pre-built APIs, code-first approach, unified data models, and enterprise-grade security. Free tier available. Alternative to Pipedream, Rube, Apideck. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/nangohq/nango)
- [OpenLIT](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/openlit) - Open-source observability platform for GenAI and LLM applications. Real-time monitoring, distributed tracing, prompt management, and AI model evaluation built on OpenTelemetry. Alternative to LangSmith, Humanloop, Weights. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/openlit/openlit)
- [OpenLLMetry](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/openllmetry) - Open-source observability platform for LLMs using OpenTelemetry. Monitor performance, track costs, and debug AI applications with just 2 lines of code. Alternative to DataDog, LangSmith, Splunk. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/traceloop/openllmetry)
- [Pipeshub](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/pipeshub) - Self-hostable enterprise AI platform that unifies business data across apps, powers a knowledge graph for cited answers, and lets teams build AI agents across their stack. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/pipeshub-ai/pipeshub-ai/)
- [Portkey AI Gateway](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/portkey-ai-gateway) - Comprehensive AI platform with gateway, observability, guardrails, and prompt management. Access 1,600+ LLMs via unified API with enterprise-grade security. Alternative to Eden AI, Vercel AI Gateway, Cloudflare AI Gateway. [`Course`](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/codex/portkey-ai-gateway) `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/portkey-ai/gateway)
- [Qdrant](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/qdrant) - Qdrant is an open-source vector database that provides high-performance similarity search for AI and machine learning applications. Alternative to Supabase, Pinecone, Algolia. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/qdrant/qdrant)
- [Rivet](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/rivet) - Open-source infrastructure for long-lived, in-memory processes called Actors. Combines state and compute with sub-millisecond latency, realtime capabilities, and horizontal scaling. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/rivet-dev/rivet)
- [Suna](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/suna) - Open source AI assistant that executes complex tasks from market research to travel planning through natural conversation, with full transparency and community-driven development. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/kortix-ai/suna)
- [Supermemory](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/supermemory) - Add persistent memory to LLM apps with millisecond recall times. Store, retrieve, and personalize user data across sessions with enterprise-grade security. Alternative to LangChain, Pinecone. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/supermemoryai/supermemory)
- [Trieve](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/trieve) - Trieve offers an all-in-one solution for search, recommendations, and RAG with automatic continuous improvement based on user feedback. Alternative to Pinecone, Algolia, ElasticSearch. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/devflowinc/trieve)
- [FauxPilot](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/fauxpilot) - FauxPilot - an open-source alternative to GitHub Copilot server Alternative to Github Copilot, Cursor. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/fauxpilot/fauxpilot)
- [YouCompleteMe](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/youcompleteme) - A code-completion & code-comprehension server Alternative to Github Copilot, Cursor. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/ycm-core/ycmd)
- [ChatRWKV](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/chatrwkv) - ChatRWKV is like ChatGPT but powered by RWKV (100% RNN) language model, and open source. Alternative to ChatGPT, Claude. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/BlinkDL/ChatRWKV)
- [OpenAssistant](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/openassistant) - OpenAssistant is a chat-based assistant that understands tasks, can interact with third-party systems, and retrieve information dynamically to do so. Alternative to ChatGPT, Claude. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/LAION-AI/Open-Assistant)
- [DashPress](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/dashpress) - Generate powerful admin apps without writing a single line of code - Run `npx dashpress` to see some magic! Alternative to Retool, Appsmith. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/dashpresshq/dashpress)
- [ILLA](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/illa) - Low-code platform allows you to build business apps, enables you to quickly create internal tools such as dashboard, crud app, admin panel, crm, cms, etc. Supports PostgreSQL, MySQL, Supabase, GraphQL, MongoDB, MSSQL, Rest API, Hugging Face, Redis, etc. Automate workflows with schedule or webhook. Open source Retool. Alternative to Retool, Appsmith. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/illacloud/illa-builder)
- [Openblocks](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/openblocks) - 🔥 🔥 🔥 The Open Source Retool Alternative Alternative to Retool, Appsmith. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/openblocks-dev/openblocks)
- [CozoDB](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/cozodb) - A transactional, relational-graph-vector database that uses Datalog for query. The hippocampus for AI! Alternative to Pinecone, Weaviate. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/cozodb/cozo)

### Machine Learning Infrastructure

- [Beam](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/beam) - Run AI workloads with sub-second cold starts, elastic GPU scaling, and secure sandboxed environments. Scale to zero when idle, burst to thousands instantly. Alternative to Together Sandbox, Vertex AI, Modal. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/beam-cloud/beta9/)
- [Daytona](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/daytona) - Elastic sandbox infrastructure for running AI-generated code with sub-90ms environment creation, stateful operations, and isolated execution across Python, TypeScript, Go, and more. Alternative to Together Sandbox, Modal, Sprites. [`Course`](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/codex/daytonaio-daytona) `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/daytonaio/daytona/)
- [Laminar](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/laminar) - Laminar is an open-source platform that helps collect, understand, and utilize data for building high-quality LLM applications. Alternative to LangChain, Pinecone. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/lmnr-ai/lmnr)
- [Letta](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/letta) - Letta is an open-source platform for creating AI agents with built-in memory, reasoning, and support for thousands of tools. Alternative to Perplexity, LangChain, Pinecone. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/letta-ai/letta)
- [Mem0](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/mem0) - Adds persistent, searchable memory to AI agents and apps, so they remember user preferences and past interactions across sessions without pipeline changes. Alternative to LangChain, Pinecone, Vertex AI. [`Course`](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/codex/mem0-ai-memory-layer) [`Classroom`](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/classrooms/7bed9716-ba55-4442-b3f3-3cbb22343d0a) [Repo](https://github.com/mem0ai/mem0)
- [OpenLIT](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/openlit) - Open-source observability platform for GenAI and LLM applications. Real-time monitoring, distributed tracing, prompt management, and AI model evaluation built on OpenTelemetry. Alternative to LangSmith, Humanloop, Weights. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/openlit/openlit)
- [Supermemory](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/supermemory) - Add persistent memory to LLM apps with millisecond recall times. Store, retrieve, and personalize user data across sessions with enterprise-grade security. Alternative to LangChain, Pinecone. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/supermemoryai/supermemory)
- [Activeloop](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/activeloop) - Deep Lake is an open-source database for storing, querying and managing complex AI data like images, audio, and embeddings. Alternative to Snowflake, Pinecone, BigQuery. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/activeloopai/deeplake)
- [Chroma](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/chroma) - Open-source vector database designed for AI applications. Store, search, and retrieve embeddings with semantic similarity matching and metadata filtering. Alternative to Supabase, Pinecone, ElasticSearch. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/chroma-core/chroma)
- [Deepnote](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/deepnote) - Deepnote is an open-source collaborative notebook for data analysts and scientists, combining Python, SQL, AI assistance, and live sharing in one cloud platform. Alternative to Snowflake, Tableau, Hex. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/deepnote/deepnote)
- [Helicone](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/helicone) - Open-source platform for logging, monitoring, and debugging LLM applications. Route, debug, and analyze AI apps with comprehensive observability tools. Alternative to DataDog, LangSmith, LangChain. [`Course`](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/codex/helicone) `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/helicone/helicone)
- [mlop](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/mlop) - Open source platform for ML engineers to track metrics, parameters, and gradients in real-time. Features Git integration, alerts, and seamless workflow integration. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/mlop-ai/mlop)
- [Weaviate](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/weaviate) - Open-source vector database designed for building powerful, production-ready AI applications with hybrid search capabilities and flexible deployment options. Alternative to Supabase, Pinecone. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/weaviate/weaviate)

### AI Security & Privacy

- [LiteLLM](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/litellm) - Acts as a unified proxy across 100+ LLMs, normalizing them to the OpenAI format while handling virtual keys, budgets, rate limits, fallbacks, and cost tracking. Alternative to LangChain, Eden AI, OpenRouter. [`Course`](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/codex/berriai-litellm) `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/berriai/litellm)
- [Proxed AI](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/proxed-ai) - A secure proxy service that protects AI API keys using Apple DeviceCheck, enabling safe integration of ChatGPT, Claude, and other AI models in iOS apps `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/nech-ai/proxed)

## Data & Analytics

### Web & Product Analytics

- [Lua.sh](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/lua-sh) - Open-source platform for creating shortened URLs with advanced analytics, custom domains, and API integration for marketing and development teams. Alternative to TinyURL, Bitly, Short.io. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/luadotsh/lua)
- [OpenPanel](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/openpanel) - Open-source analytics platform covering web traffic, custom events, funnels, retention, session replay, and revenue tracking. GDPR-compliant with optional self-hosting. Alternative to Google Analytics, Cloudflare Analytics, Mixpanel. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/openpanel-dev/openpanel)
- [Aptabase](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/aptabase) - Open-source, self-hostable analytics platform for mobile and desktop apps, prioritizing user privacy and data control. Alternative to Google Analytics, Mixpanel, Amplitude. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/aptabase/aptabase)
- [Betterlytics](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/betterlytics) - GDPR-compliant web analytics with real-time insights, session replay, and funnel tracking. No cookies, no tracking, no consent banners required. Alternative to Google Analytics, Cloudflare Analytics, Mixpanel. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/betterlytics/betterlytics)
- [Countly](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/countly) - All-in-one analytics platform for mobile, web, and desktop apps. Track user behavior, monitor performance, and optimize your product. Alternative to Google Analytics, Cloudflare Analytics, Mixpanel. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/countly/countly-server)
- [Databuddy](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/databuddy) - Get powerful web analytics with zero cookies, 100% GDPR compliance, and full data ownership. Lightweight 3KB script delivers real-time insights without compromising user privacy. Alternative to Google Analytics, Cloudflare Analytics, Mixpanel. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/databuddy-analytics/databuddy)
- [Fathom Lite](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/fathom) - A simple, privacy-first analytics platform that provides valuable website insights without compromising visitor data or requiring cookie consent banners. Alternative to Google Analytics, Cloudflare Analytics, Mixpanel. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/usefathom/fathom)
- [GrowthBook](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/growthbook) - Powerful, developer-friendly experimentation tool for data-driven product decisions. Seamless integration, real-time insights, and flexible deployment. Alternative to LaunchDarkly, Hypertune, Statsig. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/growthbook/growthbook)
- [HitKeep](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/hitkeep) - Self-hosted or managed web analytics with zero external dependencies. Cookie-free tracking, full data sovereignty, and single binary deployment for organizations that own their data. Alternative to Google Analytics, Cloudflare Analytics, Mixpanel. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/PascaleBeier/hitkeep)
- [Litlyx](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/litlyx) - Track user behavior, custom events, and conversion funnels in real-time with a single line of code, all while maintaining GDPR compliance. Alternative to Google Analytics, Cloudflare Analytics, Mixpanel. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/litlyx/litlyx)
- [Matomo](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/matomo) - Comprehensive web analytics platform offering full data ownership, privacy protection, and customizable insights for data-driven decision making. Alternative to Google Analytics, Cloudflare Analytics, Mixpanel. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/matomo-org/matomo)

### Search Engines

- [Onyx](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/onyx) - An open-source platform that connects to 40+ apps to provide intelligent search and AI assistance across all company information Alternative to Algolia, ElasticSearch, Glean. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/onyx-dot-app/onyx)

- [Elasticsearch](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/elasticsearch) - Elasticsearch is an open-source, RESTful search engine designed for scalability, reliability, and easy management. - [Manticore Search](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/manticore) - Open source search database delivering 2.83x faster performance than Elasticsearch. Features vector search, SQL interface, and full-text capabilities. Alternative to Algolia, ElasticSearch, AWS Kendra. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/manticoresoftware/manticoresearch)
- [Meilisearch](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/meilisearch) - A powerful, fast, and easy-to-use search engine that delivers instant and relevant results for your websites and applications. - [OpenSearch](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/opensearch) - Community-driven, Apache 2.0-licensed search and analytics suite for ingesting, searching, visualizing, and analyzing data at scale with AI/ML capabilities. - [Quickwit](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/quickwit) - High-performance search engine designed for big data, offering scalability, real-time indexing, and cost-effective operations. Alternative to Snowflake, MongoDB, Kdb+. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/timescale/timescaledb)
- [Turso](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/turso) - Turso provides a simple developer experience with SQLite compatibility, allowing you to build and scale multi-tenant applications with unlimited databases. - [Anthias](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/anthias) - Free open-source digital signage software that turns Raspberry Pi or old PCs into powerful display solutions. No subscription, no training required. Alternative to Wispr Flow, Superwhisper, Voiceflow. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/akshayaggarwal99/jarvis-ai-assistant)
- [OpenWispr](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/openwispr) - Dictation app powered by OpenAI Whisper and NVIDIA Parakeet. Runs locally on macOS, Windows, and Linux with zero data retention and 100+ language support. Alternative to Wispr Flow, Superwhisper, Aqua Voice. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/herotools/open-wispr)
- [VoiceInk](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/voiceink) - Convert speech to text instantly with advanced AI voice recognition. 100% private, offline capable, supports 100+ languages. Works across all Mac applications. Alternative to Wispr Flow, Superwhisper, Aqua Voice. `Course: soon` `Classroom: soon` [Repo](https://github.com/beingpax/voiceink)

## Built with AIFlowLearn

Each item can grow into a project detail page, a Codex architecture course, and an interactive classroom that carries the slide preview.
